 -agar farsh par gilaa rang abhi tak he to sabase pehle use paper towel kii madad se ponch len
 Do not leave the color on the floor for too long, otherwise it will be difficult to remove the stain
 uske baad us jagah par surf chhidakkar kuch der ke liye chhod den
 After that, rub it clean with a nylon scrubber
 -aap chahen to farsh par lage dhabbon ko baking soda or pani kii madad se bhi saaf kar sakate hai
 Prepare a paste or thick solution by mixing baking soda and water
 is ghol ko dhabbe par lagaakar kuch der ke liye chhod den

 dhabba saaf ho jayega
